<div class="flex gap-2 mb-4 flex-wrap">
<span class="inline-flex items-center px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-primary/10 text-primary-dark dark:text-primary border border-primary/20">
<span class="mr-1">#</span> 纪念日
                </span>
<span class="inline-flex items-center px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-gray-100 dark:bg-white/10 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300">
<span class="mr-1">#</span> 探店
                </span>
<span class="inline-flex items-center px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-gray-100 dark:bg-white/10 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300">
<span class="mr-1">#</span> Omakase
                </span>
</div>
<div class="prose prose-sm dark:prose-invert max-w-none text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300 leading-relaxed font-body">
<p>
                    非常惊喜的一次用餐体验。食材极其新鲜，大腹入口即化，海胆鲜甜没有任何腥味。主厨很健谈，介绍了每一道菜的来源和设计思路。
                </p>
<p class="mt-2">
                    环境私密性很好，只有八个板前座位，很适合我们这次的三周年纪念日。最后送的手作甜品也是点睛之笔。仿佛一秒回到了京都的那个夏天。🍃
                </p>
<p class="mt-3 text-xs text-gray-400 font-display flex items-center gap-1">
<span class="material-icons-round text-[14px]">schedule</span>
                    记录于 2023年10月15日 19:30
                </p>

<h1 class="text-3xl font-bold mb-4 text-slate-800 dark:text-white font-body leading-tight tracking-tight">遇见秋日的小确幸</h1>
<p class="text-lg leading-relaxed text-slate-600 dark:text-slate-300 font-body text-justify mb-6">
            今天路过花店，被橱窗里那一抹灿烂的金黄吸引。没忍住买了一束向日葵，抱在怀里的时候，仿佛拥抱了整个秋天的阳光。心情瞬间变得明亮起来，连路边的梧桐树叶都显得格外温柔。原来快乐可以这么简单，只要一束花就够了。🌻
        </p>
<div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-2">
<span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-orange-50 dark:bg-orange-900/20 text-orange-500 dark:text-orange-400 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full text-sm font-semibold border border-orange-100 dark:border-orange-900/30">
<span class="material-icons-round text-sm">wb_sunny</span>
<span>治愈 · Healing</span>
</span>

<span>花店偶遇</span>
</span>
